<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I was referred to Bay Area Endodontics because I was in need of a root canal on tooth#3 and the dentist I saw felt that I needed to be referred to a Specialist to have the procedure done because it was not going to be an easy RCT.  I referred to another practice first but found out after I spoke with them that they were not in my insurance network.  My dentist office called me back and advised that I can go to Bay Area Endodontics.  I first want to say that I had never had a root canal before so the only thing I knew about them is what I had heard from other people who had one done and I heard nothing but horror stories.  I was a little hesitant when I called in to schedule my appointment because I cannot handle tooth pain AT ALL.  I called in and originally scheduled my appointment for 6/1 in their San Mateo location.  I had asked if they had an opening sooner if they could let me know.  Well literally 10 minutes after I scheduled for 6/1, I received a call that they just had a cancellation so I could come in the very same day later on at 12:45pm.  It was 9am when I was on the phone with them.  They emailed me the paperwork I needed to fill out, called me before my appointment to let me know how much my out of pocket amount would be.  They also advised that if I needed to make payment arrangements I would be able to talk to them about it when I came in.  Now on to the BEST part of this review....I arrived right at 1pm and was called back within 10 minutes of me arriving.  They took X-rays and explained everything they were doing IN DETAIL and the lovely part of this was the fact that I DID NOT FEEL ANY PAIN AT ALL.  I heard the drilling and whatever else was going on but I didn't feel a single thing.  It was AMAZING.  In addition to not feeling a single thing, I was back home by 2:25pm.   The numbness was gone by 4pm and I did not need to take Tylenol or Ibuprophen because I didn't feel any pain at all.  I  just want to THANK everyone at Bay Area Endodontics for being AWESOME!  I will be referring anyone I know who is in need of a root canal to them.  They were  absolutely WONDERFUL!  From the scheduler, to the girl at the front desk to the actual Endodontist and the Hygenist Nancy.  I believe she is a Hygenist but not sure.  Anyways, they are absolutely AMAZING!!!  If I could give them 10 stars I would.<//review>

108592397375994544608<//user>
<text>So this place is supposed to be based off Chicago style offerings and the menu looks delightful as far as Chicago food staples. I love Chicago and the food there is amazing but one of my all time favorites is the Italian beef sandwich.

I ordered the "Hella Big Beef" and when it came out, it resembles an authentic Chicago style beef sammy. Unfortunately, it did not taste like Chicago's. It was decent but nothing beats the real deal.

My wife ordered the "Chicago Authentic" hot dog and I must say, it tasted like those in Chicago. Right down to the bright green pickle relish. A hot is a hot dog though.

The sides however were great. We ordered the truffle fries and the fried zucchini. The fries were thick cut and not the shoestring style and it is a large serving. The zucchini is cut into french fry style and fried to crispy perfection.

I will not be frequenting this place or raving about it but it is a cool lil spot for a quick bite.<//text></record></dataset><record>

<Review>Here‚Äôs the thing about steakhouses in Las Vegas: every major hotel and casino has one... and most of ‚Äòem are really, really good. (And that‚Äôs not to mention all the ones that aren‚Äôt in a hotel or casino.) Deciding on the perfect place to sink your teeth into a tender piece of meat can be tough. If somebody would just put together a complete guide to Sin City‚Äôs best steak spots... oh, wait! My bad ....
We are in Pines Modern Steakhouse at the San Manuel Casino.
Savor the flavors and freshness of delicious and unprecedented cuisine in the modern sophistication and elegance of this remodeled Venue.

Dine from a revamped and updated dinner menu featuring cutting-edge flavors and dishes. The menu features organic and locally sourced produce with an exclusive brand of some of the most sought after WAGYU BEEF on the planet. and the freshest and finest seafood delivered daily. The Pines Steakhouse will create a delectable dining experience unparalleled in the Inland Empire.

An extensive wine list housing some of the world‚Äôs most magnificent wines has been crafted to complement the flavors and excitement of the extraordinary new menu.

This energetic fine dining spot could be the best reason to visit Southern California just for the STEAKS!
What sets it apart: You might be getting the best-prepared steaks in the World never mind the good ole USA. Snow Beef? Are you kidding me ?  No I am not actually for those of you do not know about Snow Beef here is some great information.
The Japanese Black Wagyu cattle are raised at Chateau Uenae Lake Farm, a private reserve in Hokkaido, which is the northernmost part of Japan where it gets very cold. The cold climate is what creates the unique meat quality and allows the beef to become as delicate as a snowflake, thus the name Snow Beef.

With only one to two cattle per month qualifying for Chateau Uenae's top designation, Hokkaido "Snow Beef" is the rarest steak on the planet. Its also happens to be the best steak we've ever have tasted prepared with precise perfection.
With robust yet incredibly delicate marbling, this is Special, Chic, Majestic and a Graceful Cut of Beef.
As an avid foodie I have never ever seen this jewel on any menu including Japan..
The Service is impeccable, The Ambiance is Warm, The Food is Outrageous and there WAGYU BEEF is a mouth watering experience.<//Review>< pictures>

<userid>103903454811920446621</userid><Name>Leticia Sanchez</Name><Date>1485057383840</Date>< rate>

< Review>
Had a Great time with My husband last night!! I never take the time to write reviews, but we promised our server Jack that we would because we had such a great time.

The Pines is a beautiful restaurant with modern twist and elegant decor. The only complaint I have is the fact that they don't have a restroom in house!! So you are forced to go back out onto the casino floor into a cloud of second hand smoke and unpleasant loud noises.

When we entered the Pines the nice hostesses greeted us courteously however we would have rather sat at a booth instead of a small table for 2 where one of us had to sit with our back facing the live band that they had to offer. The menus were extremely fancy all of their menus were made of an extravagant wood finish.But we were greeted warmly by our server Jack, an extremely charming and professional(very good looking as well) young man that made up for it. He was able to offer me my favorite Cakebread Chardonnay at a discounted price ($70 for an entire bottle!!!what a bargain) he walked us through the menu and set us up with a 3 course meal that complimented the wine wonderfully. The food was fantastic, both my husbands ribeye and my burger were cooked to perfection, hats off to the chef.  He stopped by to check on us often,  and made sure that we tried their house made steak sauces, and had everything we needed through the entire meal.  Even though we could see he had several other tables and was quite busy. I especially loved the way he served out wine, the way her poured each glass was SUPER CLASSY.

If you ever find yourself around the Highland area looking for a great dining experience I Would definitely recommend making your way over to the pines. The place is a bit pricy but, definitely worth it, if you want to  spoil you and your hubby with. And make sure you ask for Jack!!</Review>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><user>105692744256480109238< /user><response>{'time': 1469720957449, 'text': 'Chelsea -\n\nThanks for the feedback and the five stars! This is one of he most thorough and intelligent reviews we have ever read. Well done!\n\nWe cannot wait to host you again soon!\n-San Manuel Casino'}<//response>< review>
Your dinner starts with a bread service of cheesy herb pull-apart rolls served in a cast-iron skillet. Get your hands on one before they disappear! Your dining mate may fight you for them. They are so good! Rating: 4.9/5

Hurricane ($12) features their own blend of fresh fruits and Zaya Rum and is served in a frosted tiki glass. If you have ever been to Pat O‚ÄôBriens in New Orleans, you will absolutely love The Pines version. It is tropical in flavor yet packs a punch with the Zaya Rum. Rating: 5/5

Crab Cakes ($18) are made with jumbo lump crab and roasted red pepper, and served with a creole remoulade and mango foam. The crab cakes are amazing! Lots of crab meat and not a lot of filler. The only thing that doesn‚Äôt really match is the mango foam. The flavor is too sweet and seemed to overpower the delicate, succulent flavor of the crab. Sample a little first before utilizing it on the crab cakes. Rating: 4.7/5

Veal Meatballs ($12) are served with organic Pomodoro, parmigiana reggiano, and basil. The sauce has an excellent balance of sweet and savory. But the veal may be a little too delicate of a flavor for the bold sauce. Maybe a mix of veal and beef or pork and beef might be better to lend its flavor to the mix. Rating: 4.3/5

Farmer‚Äôs Market Salad made with certified 100% organic kales, California oranges, extra virgin olive oil (EVOO), and sherry. This is a refreshing salad for summer, but instead of grapefruit, blood orange might be a better citrus fruit to use. It will provide contrast with the deep green kale in both presentation and flavor. The bitterness in the grapefruit enhanced too much of the bitterness of the kale. Rating: 4/5

Longbone Ribeye ($80) is a 32 oz. bone-in steak that will inspire ‚Äúoohs‚Äù and ‚Äúahhs‚Äù not only from the table, but from the entire restaurant as it carried through the dining room from the kitchen. An extra length of frenched bone is served with this ribeye. The steak is tender, juicy, flavorful, and perfectly grilled to your liking. It could use a tad more salt on the grill. Rating: 4.7/5

Prime Rib ($32 for 12 oz. or $38 for 16 oz.) is traditionally served with au jus and creamed horseradish. It is tender, juicy, and seasoned to perfection. The perfect temperature cut is selected just for you. The au jus is full of rich beef flavor. The horseradish is well-balanced with a creamy and spicy kick. Rating: 4.8/5

Cold Water Lobster Tail (market price) can be served either steamed or broiled. If you choose broiled option, a garlic butter is added to the lobster. It is broiled to perfection with succulent buttery flavor. The garlic works really well with the sweet lobster. Rating: 5/5

Red King Crab Legs (market price) can be served steamed or garlic roasted. If you choose the steamed option, the crab meat is perfectly steamed and served in sections for easy removal. The meat comes out cleanly indicating the crab is very fresh. Rating: 4.7/5

Signature Mashed Potatoes ($10) are like a twice-baked potato without the skin and mixed with bacon, cheese, and chives. The cheesy bacon flavor pairs well with the mash. The potatoes are very dense. It might be better whipped to provide a lighter consistency. Rating: 4.3/5

Cannoli ($8) is artfully filled and the ends are dipped in chocolate. Pistachio and mocha almond fillings were served. The ends are dotted with almonds and pistachios and sprinkled with powdered sugar.  The cannoli shells are perfectly crisp. The fillings are creamy and rich with flavors of pistachio, chocolate, and coffee. Mama mia! Rating: 5/5

Pines Chocolate ‚ÄúPeak‚Äù ($8) is an amazing dessert to share, especially if you are celebrating birthday or anniversary. The inside is a wedge of chocolate layered cake flipped up to make a ‚Äúmountain peak‚Äù. It is encased in a chocolate shell and the ‚Äúpeak‚Äù is sprinkled with powdered sugar to emulate snow. It will pull at the heartstrings of any chocoholic! Rating: 5/5< /review>

This is a gluten free review.

Gluten free menu: No, but GF items clearly marked

What I ordered: Karate Chicken with Buttload‚Äôa Fries (this is a funny item to order. Feels weird to say it lol)

Gluten free options: 5/5
The whole menu is gluten free

Food: 3/5
The chicken and fries are HOT and fresh. I‚Äôm not a huge fan of the Tastea dust. This seasoning is very strong. I wish it was a little less overwhelming. Both the fries and nuggets are very ‚Äúheavy‚Äù. I can usually only eat about half of it before I feel like I need a salad or something healthy. There‚Äôs not a lot of places where you can have gluten free chicken nuggets in Orange County (I know of two places).

The smoothies and teas are awesome. So much variety. I especially love the summer flavors.

Service: 4/5

Ambiance: 2/5

Price: 4/5
Prices are reasonable.

Purchased a rim and tire package and was set to come in the next day to get it installed. While doing some research online, I found a better rim with a better offset for my vehicle and was willing to pay the difference to get these rims instead. I assumed it wouldn't be a problem since the shop is a distributor for the same company of the rim. Called the next day and they said they only are distributors for the tires of the brand, not the rims. I said no problem, I will order the rims and still get the tires since they are the same brand and I wanted them to match. They no longer wanted my business because they weren't profiting from me sourcing the rims myself and they wouldn't assist in helping me get them, only offered a refund since I paid in advance. Even said to get the tires somewhere else too, and that's exactly what I did. Took my business elsewhere. If I'm spending almost 2 G's, I have every right to change my mind on what I want, just like you have the right to refuse my business because you got mad I wanted a different rim and it was going to eat into your profit margin. I went to STW in La Habra and they made some calls and sourced the rims for me next day. People can make there own conclusion from this review.</Review>
